political_decisions = {	
	##########################
	### MILITARY DECISIONS ###
	##########################
	
	#Hide/Show Military Decisions
	hide_military_decisions = {
		picture = "hide_military_decisions"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
		}
		
		allow = { war = no }
		
		effect = {
			set_country_flag = hide_military_decisions
		}
		
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 0
		}
		
	}
	show_military_decisions = {
		picture = "show_military_decisions"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions
		}
		
		allow = { }
		
		effect = {
			clr_country_flag = hide_military_decisions
		}
		
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	defcon1_decision = {
		picture = "defcon1"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			ai = no
			is_vassal = no
			has_country_modifier = defcon2
		}

		alert = no

		allow = {
			OR = { war_policy = jingoism war = yes involved_in_crisis = yes }
		}

		effect = {

			random_province = { limit = { owner = { crisis_exist = yes involved_in_crisis = yes has_country_modifier = defcon2 } } owner = { add_crisis_temperature = 10 } }

			remove_country_modifier = defcon5
			remove_country_modifier = defcon4
			remove_country_modifier = defcon3
			remove_country_modifier = defcon2
			remove_country_modifier = defcon1
			add_country_modifier = { name = defcon1 duration = -1 }
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	defcon2_decision = {
		picture = "defcon2"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			ai = no
			is_vassal = no
			OR = { has_country_modifier = defcon1 has_country_modifier = defcon3 }
		}

		alert = no

		allow = {
			OR = { war_policy = jingoism war = yes involved_in_crisis = yes war = no }
		}

		effect = {

			random_province = { limit = { owner = { crisis_exist = yes involved_in_crisis = yes has_country_modifier = defcon3 } } owner = { add_crisis_temperature = 10 } }

			remove_country_modifier = defcon5
			remove_country_modifier = defcon4
			remove_country_modifier = defcon3
			remove_country_modifier = defcon2
			remove_country_modifier = defcon1
			add_country_modifier = { name = defcon2 duration = -1 }
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	defcon3_decision = {
		picture = "defcon3"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			ai = no
			is_vassal = no
			OR = { has_country_modifier = defcon2 has_country_modifier = defcon4 }
		}

		alert = no

		allow = {

			OR = { 
				war = no 
				AND = { war = no has_country_modifier = defcon2 }
			}

			OR = { 
				war_policy = jingoism 
				war_policy = pro_military 
				war = yes 
				involved_in_crisis = yes 
				AND = { has_country_modifier = defcon2 war_policy = pacifism } 
				AND = { has_country_modifier = defcon1 war_policy = pacifism } 
				AND = { war = no has_country_modifier = defcon2 }
			}
		}

		effect = {

			random_province = { limit = { owner = { crisis_exist = yes involved_in_crisis = yes has_country_modifier = defcon4 } } owner = { add_crisis_temperature = 10 } }

			remove_country_modifier = defcon5
			remove_country_modifier = defcon4
			remove_country_modifier = defcon3
			remove_country_modifier = defcon2
			remove_country_modifier = defcon1
			add_country_modifier = { name = defcon3 duration = -1 }
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
				factor = 1
		}
	}

	reset_bomb = {
		picture = "reset_bomb"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			OR = { has_country_modifier = atomic_nation has_country_modifier = hydrogen_nation }
			OR = { 
				has_country_flag = icbm_bomb
				has_country_flag = sub_bomb 
				has_country_flag = air_bomb 
				has_country_modifier = tactical_nukes 
			}
		}

		allow = {
			war = no
			OR = { 
				ai = no 
				AND = { ai = yes is_greater_power = no is_secondary_power = no has_country_flag = icbm_bomb has_country_flag = sub_bomb }
				AND = { ai = yes is_greater_power = no has_country_flag = icbm_bomb }
			} 
		}

		effect = {
			clr_country_flag = icbm_bomb
			clr_country_flag = sub_bomb
			clr_country_flag = air_bomb

			remove_country_modifier = tactical_nukes
		}

	}
	air_bomb = {
		picture = "air_bomb"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			strategic_bomber = 1
			OR = { has_country_modifier = atomic_nation has_country_modifier = hydrogen_nation }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = air_bomb }
		}

		allow = {
			military_score = 600
		}

		effect = {
			set_country_flag = air_bomb
		}
	}
	sub_bomb = {
		picture = "sub_bomb"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			submarine_launched_ballistic_missile = 1
			OR = { has_country_modifier = atomic_nation has_country_modifier = hydrogen_nation }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = sub_bomb }
			
			num_of_ports = 1
		}

		allow = {
			num_of_ports = 1

			OR = { is_greater_power = yes is_secondary_power = yes }
			
			military_score = 600
		}

		effect = {
			set_country_flag = sub_bomb	
		}
	}
	icbm_bomb = {
		picture = "icbm_bomb"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			icbm = 1
			OR = { has_country_modifier = atomic_nation has_country_modifier = hydrogen_nation }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = icbm_bomb }
		}

		allow = {
			military_score = 600
			invention = second_generation_icbm
			is_greater_power = yes
		}

		effect = {
			set_country_flag = icbm_bomb 
		}
	}

	changeabm = {
		picture = "changeabm"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = abm_treaty }
			has_country_modifier = sdi_completed
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = abm_timer }
			has_country_flag = abm_school
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = abmhigh
				has_country_modifier = abmmedium
				has_country_modifier = abmlow
			}
		}
		
		alert = no
		
		allow = {
			election = no
			OR = { ai = no AND = { NOT = { badboy = 0.25 } money = 5000000 } }

			OR = { 
				ai = no 
				AND = { 
					has_country_modifier = abmhigh 
					NOT = { money = 40000000 } 
				}

				AND = { 
					has_country_modifier = abmmedium 
					NOT = { 
						AND = { NOT = { money = 40000000 } money = 20000000 } 
					}
				}

				AND = { has_country_modifier = abmlow money = 20000000 }

			}

		}
		effect = {
			remove_country_modifier = abmhigh
			remove_country_modifier = abmmedium
			remove_country_modifier = abmlow
			clr_country_flag = abmhigh
			clr_country_flag = abmmedium
			clr_country_flag = abmlow
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	abmhigh = {
		picture = "abmhigh"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = abm_treaty }
			has_country_flag = abm_school
			has_country_modifier = sdi_completed
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = abm_timer }
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = abmhigh
					has_country_modifier = abmmedium
					has_country_modifier = abmlow
				}
			}
		}
		allow = {

			OR = { ai = no money = 40000000 }

			OR = { ai = no NOT = { badboy = 0.25 } }

		}

		effect = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = abmhigh duration = -1 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = abm_timer duration = 1850 }

			money = -2000000
			badboy = 10
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	reset_chemical_bomb = {
		picture = "reset_chemical_bomb"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			has_country_modifier = chemical_nation
			OR = { has_country_flag = nerve_bomb has_country_flag = blister_bomb has_country_flag = choking_bomb }
		}
		
		alert = no

		allow = {
			election = no

				ai = no 

				AND = { NOT = { money = 1000000 } has_country_flag = nerve_bomb }

				AND = { NOT = { money = 750000 } has_country_flag = blister_bomb }
			}
			
		}

		effect = {

			clr_country_flag = blister_bomb
		}

	changecd = {
		picture = "changecd"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = nuke_shelters_activate }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = cd_timer }
			mutual_assured_destruction = 1
			OR = { has_country_modifier = cdhigh
			has_country_modifier = cdmedium
			has_country_modifier = cdlow }
		}
		alert = no
		allow = {
			election = no
			OR = {
				ai = no
				AND = {
					ai = yes
					OR = { 
						AND = { 
							has_country_modifier = cdhigh 
							NOT = { 
								OR = {
									AND = { ai = yes has_country_modifier = defcon1 war = yes }
									AND = { ai = yes war_policy = jingoism war = no }
									war = yes
								}
							} 
						} 
						AND = { 
							has_country_modifier = cdmedium 
							NOT = { AND = { ai = yes war_policy = pro_military war = no } } 
						} 
						AND = { 
							has_country_modifier = cdlow
							NOT = { AND = { ai = yes war_policy = pacifism war = no } } 
						} 
					}
				}
			} 
		}
		effect = {		
			remove_country_modifier = cdhigh
			remove_country_modifier = cdmedium
			remove_country_modifier = cdlow
			clr_country_flag = cdhigh
			clr_country_flag = cdmedium
			clr_country_flag = cdlow
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 100 
		}
	}

	war_bonds_issue = {
		picture = "war_bonds"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			war = yes
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = war_bonds }
			NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist }
		}
		allow = {
			is_mobilised = yes
			OR = { ai = no NOT = { money = 50000 } }		
		}
		effect = {
			war_exhaustion = 5
			add_country_modifier = { name = war_bonds duration = 365 }
			any_owned = { 
				limit = { is_core = THIS } 
				owner = { money = 500 } 
			}
			#Lower class
			farmers = { money = -2 }
			labourers = { money = -2 }
			craftsmen = { money = -2 }
			#Middle class
			clergymen = { money = -5 }
			clerks = { money = -5 }
			#Business class
			capitalists = { money = -10 }
			aristocrats = { money = -10 }
			artisans = { money = -10 }
			#Military gets more money
			soldiers = { money = 10 }
			officers = { money = 20 }
			#Government gets more money
			bureaucrats = { money = 10 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

	start_strategic_bombardment = {
		picture = "strategic_bombardment"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_military_decisions }
			war = yes
			is_vassal = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = strategic_bombardment }
			has_country_flag = aerial_bombardment_ability
			
			#Must have allies near the war country
			war_countries = { 
				neighbour = THIS 
				any_neighbor_country = { 
					OR = { 
						in_sphere = THIS 
						alliance_with = THIS 
						military_access = THIS
					} 
				}
			}
		}
		alert = no
		allow = {
			OR = { 
				NOT = { war_policy = pacifism } 
				war_exhaustion = 50 
			}
			military_score = 500
		}

		effect = {
			prestige = -25
			badboy = 5
			set_country_flag = strategic_bombardment
			
			#Bomb a random country's capital
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					war_with = THIS 
					capital_scope = { 
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = aerial_bombed } 
						NOT = { controlled_by = THIS }
					}
				}
				country_event = 124101
			}
				
				
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0 badboy = 0.8 }
		}
			
	}

	develop_vaccine = {
		picture = "develop_vaccine"
		alert = yes
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			OR = { has_country_flag = enable_virus_controls has_country_modifier = biological_attack }
			OR = { has_global_flag = epidemic_start has_country_modifier = biological_attack }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = vaccine_development }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = vaccine_development }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = vaccine_created }
			
			#Non GPs buy vaccine once a GP creates a vaccine
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					is_greater_power = no
					any_greater_power = { has_country_modifier = vaccine_created }
				}
			}

		}

		allow = {
			money = 1000000
		}

		effect = {
			money = -500000
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_country_modifier = { name = vaccine_development duration = 300 } }
				1 = { add_country_modifier = { name = vaccine_development duration = 400 } }
				1 = { add_country_modifier = { name = vaccine_development duration = 500 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = vaccine_development
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	reform_the_local_government = {
        picture = "kaitakushi"
        alert = yes
        potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			war = no
            civilized = yes
            any_owned_province = {
                any_core = {
                    exists = no
                    capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS }
					
					# Both are necessary to check for as they will impact whether or not the non-existent nation will become democratic or stay a dictatorship thanks to clean_up.txt in events
                    OR = { # Vote franchise reforms
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { vote_franschise = none_voting } # No Voting
                            THIS = { vote_franschise = none_voting }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { vote_franschise = harassed_voting } # Harassment
                            THIS = { vote_franschise = harassed_voting }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { vote_franschise = rigged_voting } # Vote Rigging
                            THIS = { vote_franschise = rigged_voting }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { vote_franschise = gerrymandered_voting } # Gerrymandering
                            THIS = { vote_franschise = gerrymandered_voting }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { vote_franschise = free_voting } # Fair and Square
                            THIS = { vote_franschise = free_voting }
                        }
                    }
                    OR = { # Political Party Reforms
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { political_parties = parties_not_allowed } # Underground Only
                            THIS = { political_parties = parties_not_allowed }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { political_parties = parties_restricted } # Rigged Campaigning
                            THIS = { political_parties = parties_restricted }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { political_parties = parties_rigged } # Restricted Campaigning
                            THIS = { political_parties = parties_rigged }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { political_parties = parties_short } # Short Campaigning
                            THIS = { political_parties = parties_short }
                        }
                        AND =  {
                            NOT = { political_parties = parties_fair } # Fair Campaigning
                            THIS = { political_parties = parties_fair }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        allow = { war = no }

        effect = {

			#Vote Franchise
            random_owned = {
                limit = { owner = { vote_franschise = none_voting } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = none_voting
                }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { owner = { vote_franschise = harassed_voting } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = harassed_voting
                }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { owner = { vote_franschise = rigged_voting } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = rigged_voting
                }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { owner = { vote_franschise = gerrymandered_voting } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = gerrymandered_voting
                }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { owner = { vote_franschise = free_voting } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = free_voting
                }
            }

			#Upper House
			random_owned = { # Ruling Party Only
                limit = { owner = { political_opinions = ruling_party_opinion } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = ruling_party_opinion
                }
            }
			random_owned = { # Semi-Appointed
                limit = { owner = { political_opinions = appointed_opinion } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = appointed_opinion
                }
            }
			random_owned = { # Qualified State Elections
                limit = { owner = { political_opinions = semi_democratic_state_opinion } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = semi_democratic_state_opinion
                }
            }
			random_owned = { # Open State Assembly
                limit = { owner = { political_opinions = democratic_state_opinion } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = democratic_state_opinion
                }
            }
			random_owned = { # Based on Population
                limit = { owner = { political_opinions = popular_opinion } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = popular_opinion
                }
            }

			#Meetings
            random_owned = {
                limit = { owner = { public_meetings = no_meetings } }
                any_country = {
                    limit = { exists = no capital_scope = { owned_by = THIS } }
                    political_reform = no_meetings
                }
            }

	decolonise_yes = {
		picture = "decolonise_yes"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			OR = { 
				tag = BEL
				tag = NET
				tag = POR
				tag = SPA
				tag = USA
				tag = FRA
				tag = NZL
				tag = AST
				tag = ENG
				tag = IMP
				tag = FBU
			}

			OR = { 
				ai = no
				minorities_reform = minorities_oppression
			}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = decolonise_yes }


		}

		allow = {
			election = no
			OR = {
				ai = no
				tag = FBU
				ruling_party_ideology = populist
				ruling_party_ideology = nationalist
				ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist
				AND = {
					tag = FRA
					OR = { war_with = ALG ALG = { exists = no } }
				}
			}
		}

		effect = {
			set_country_flag = decolonise_yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	decolonise_no = {
		picture = "decolonise_no"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			has_country_flag = decolonise_yes
			any_owned_province = { is_colonial = yes has_province_modifier = decolonise_yes }
		}

		allow = {
			election = no

			OR = { 
				ai = no
				NOT = { minorities_reform = minorities_oppression }
			}

				ai = no
				ruling_party_ideology = liberal
				ruling_party_ideology = progressive
				ruling_party_ideology = communist
				ruling_party_ideology = communist_social
			}

		}

		alert = no

		effect = {
			clr_country_flag = decolonise_yes
			any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = decolonise_yes }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0 tag = FBU }
			modifier = { factor = 0 AND = { tag = FRA OR = { war_with = ALG ALG = { exists = no } } } }
		}

	#Locks in current national values
	entrench_national_values = {
		picture = "entrench_national_values"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = entrench_national_values_flag }
			is_vassal = no
		}
		allow = {
			election = no
			war = no
			
			#Did not recently amend the constitution
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = changecentral }
			
			OR = {
				
				#Order
				AND = {
					nationalvalue = nv_order
					OR = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist }
					OR = {
						upper_house = { ideology = conservative value = 0.67 }
						upper_house = { ideology = nationalist value = 0.67 }
						upper_house = { ideology = populist value = 0.67 }
					}
				}
				
				#Liberty
				AND = {
					nationalvalue = nv_liberty
					ruling_party_ideology = liberal
					upper_house = { ideology = liberal value = 0.67 }
				}
				
				#Equality
				AND = {
					nationalvalue = nv_equality
					OR = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social }
					OR = {
						upper_house = { ideology = socialist value = 0.67 }
						upper_house = { ideology = communist value = 0.67 }
						upper_house = { ideology = communist_social value = 0.67 }
					}
				}
				
				#Tradition
				AND = {
					nationalvalue = nv_islamic
					ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist
					upper_house = { ideology = traditionalist value = 0.67 }
				}
				
				#Meritocracy
				AND = {
					nationalvalue = nv_meritocracy
					ruling_party_ideology = big_tent
					upper_house = { ideology = big_tent value = 0.67 }
				}
				
				#Progressivism
				AND = {
					nationalvalue = nv_progressivism
					ruling_party_ideology = progressive
					upper_house = { ideology = progressive value = 0.67 }
				}
				
			}

		}
		effect = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = changecentral duration = 365 }
		
			set_country_flag = entrench_national_values_flag
			
			#Increase militancy and consciousness amongst the opposition
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = traditionalist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = conservative } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = liberal } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = big_tent } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = progressive } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = socialist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = communist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = communist_social } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = communist_social } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = nationalist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 3 ideology = populist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 3 ideology = populist } } } }
			
		}

	martial_law_civil_start = {
		picture = "martial_law_civil_starrt"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 government = socialist_democracy government = colonial_government government = mandate_government government = sar_government }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = martial_law }
			war = no
		}

		alert = no

		allow = {
	
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = martial_law_timer }

			NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive ruling_party_ideology = liberal } }

			election = no

			OR = {
				ai = no
				revolt_percentage = 0.10
			}
			OR = {
				ai = no
				average_militancy = 6
			}

		}

		effect = {
	
			#State of Emergency lasts a minimum of 2 months
			add_country_modifier = { name = martial_law_minimum_timer duration = 60 }
	
			#Clear slowdown flag for more UH support event
			clr_country_flag = i_love_democracy

			### State of Emergency benefits ###
			remove_country_modifier = law_changed_by_force

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = conservative value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = big_tent value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = socialist value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = traditionalist value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = populist value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = nationalist value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = progressive value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = liberal value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = communist value = 0.50 } }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = communist_social value = 0.50 } }
			}

			### State of Emergency cons ###
			prestige_factor = -0.01

			#Supreme Court intervention - Vassal
			random_owned = { 
				limit = { 
					owner = { 
						is_vassal = yes 
						NOT = { average_militancy = 3 }
						NOT = { revolt_percentage = 0.10 }
						OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 government = socialist_democracy government = colonial_government government = mandate_government government = sar_government } 
					} 
				} 
				owner = { country_event = 1610071 }
			}

			#Supreme Court intervention - Non vassal
			random_owned = { 
				limit = { 
					owner = { 
						is_vassal = no 
						NOT = { average_militancy = 6 }
						NOT = { any_owned_province = { is_core = THIS controlled_by_rebels = yes } }
						OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 government = socialist_democracy government = colonial_government government = mandate_government government = sar_government }
					} 
				} 
				owner = { country_event = 1610071 }
			}

			#Martial Law instigates nationalist movements in vassals
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { is_vassal = yes NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = 0.2 value = nationalist } } } }

			#Clear any existing flags
			clr_country_flag = return_to_free_meetings
			clr_country_flag = return_to_limited_meetings

			clr_country_flag = return_to_responsible_publishing
			clr_country_flag = return_to_unregulated_publishing
			clr_country_flag = return_to_firewall_publishing


			#What meeting laws to revert back to
			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { public_meetings = free_meetings } }
				owner = { political_reform = no_meetings set_country_flag = return_to_free_meetings }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { public_meetings = limited_meetings } }
				owner = { political_reform = no_meetings set_country_flag = return_to_limited_meetings }
			}

			#What press laws to revert back to
			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { publishing_rights = responsible_publishing } }
				owner = { political_reform = state_publishing set_country_flag = return_to_responsible_publishing }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { publishing_rights = free_publishing } }
				owner = { political_reform = state_publishing set_country_flag = return_to_unregulated_publishing }
			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { publishing_rights = censored_publishing } }
				owner = { political_reform = state_publishing set_country_flag = return_to_firewall_publishing }
			}

			add_country_modifier = { name = martial_law duration = -1 }

			random_list = {
				75 = { any_pop = { militancy = -4 } }
				25 = { any_pop = { militancy = -2 } }
			}

		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0 war_policy = pacifism }
		}
	}

				limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = return_to_responsible_publishing  } }

			ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist
		}
		effect = {
			tech_school = traditional_academic
			clr_country_flag = set_tech_school
			add_country_modifier = { name = national_confusion duration = 730 }
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}
	}
	switch_to_traditional_academic = { #Reset research priorities
		picture = "switch_to_traditional_academic"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }

				tech_school = industrial_tech_school

			NOT = { has_country_modifier = national_confusion }
			OR = {
				tech_school = naval_tech_school
				AND = { tech_school = army_tech_school NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist } } } 
				AND = { tech_school = culture_tech_school NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } } 
				AND = { tech_school = commerce_tech_school NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } } 
				AND = { tech_school = industrial_tech_school NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } 
				AND = { tech_school = traditional_academic NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
			}
		}
		effect = {
			set_country_flag = set_tech_school
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	population_growth = {
		alert = yes
		picture = "population_growth"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = contraception_decay }
			OR = {  #Not stable population after demographic crunch unless a nuclear war happened and nations need to repopuplate
				NOT = { has_country_flag = demographic_transition_stage_6_flag }
				has_global_flag = nuclear_war
			}
		}

		allow = {
			#Favourable local conditions
			has_recently_lost_war = no
			war = no
			election = no
			NOT = { average_militancy = 3 }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = fertility_timer }
			
			#Must have money to spend
			money = 100000

			#Right-wing ruling parties with right-wing ideologies only for AI countries
			OR = {
				ai = no
				OR = {
					AND = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist }
					AND = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = nationalist }
					AND = { ruling_party_ideology = populist pop_majority_ideology = populist }
				}
			}
			#AI
			OR = {
				ai = no
				#Expansionist nations will take this decision
				AND = { war_policy = jingoism is_disarmed = no }
				#Nations facing a demographic crunch will take this
				has_country_modifier = demographic_crunch
			}

		}

		effect = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = fertility_timer duration = 3650 } # to prevent decision spam
			add_country_modifier = { name = contraception_decay duration = 1825 } # for cleanup mechanic
		
			#Accepted pops are happy
			any_pop = { 
				limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } 
				consciousness = 5 
			}
			
			#Oppressed pops are not happy
			any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } consciousness = 5 militancy = 5 }
			
			#Decision comes with public housing reforms and child care reforms
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { public_housing_reform = low_public_housing } }
				owner = { social_reform = acceptable_public_housing }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { public_housing_reform = minimal_public_housing } }
				owner = { social_reform = low_public_housing }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { public_housing_reform = no_public_housing } }
				owner = { social_reform = minimal_public_housing }
			}
			
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { child_care = adequate_child_care } }
				owner = { social_reform = good_child_care }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { child_care = limited_child_care } }
				owner = { social_reform = adequate_child_care }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { child_care = no_child_care } }
				owner = { social_reform = limited_child_care }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		
	}

				limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = gridlocked_legislature } }

					clr_country_flag = gridlocked_legislature

				}

			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }

			}

			random_owned = { 
				limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }

			}

			}

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = liberal } scaled_militancy = { factor = 0.5 ideology = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = big_tent } scaled_militancy = { factor = 0.5 ideology = big_tent } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = communist_social } scaled_militancy = { factor = 0.5 ideology = communist_social } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist_social } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = middle } ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = middle } ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = nationalist } } } }

	#Campaign for business's interests
	campaigning_business = {
		picture = "campaigning_business"

		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			has_country_flag = show_campaigning_decision
			ai = no
			
			#Democracies only
			OR = { government = socialist_democracy government = democracy government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 government = sar_government government = colonial_government government = mandate_government }
			
			#Has the required pop type
			OR = { has_pop_type = capitalists has_pop_type = artisans has_pop_type = aristocrats }
			
			#Special ideology limitations
			NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } }
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
			election = yes
		}
		effect = {
		
			#Timer
			add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 31 }
			
			#Socialists get angry
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 1
					ideology = socialist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 3
					ideology = communist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = communist_social
				}
			}
			
			#Boost ideology support
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = capitalists type = artisans type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist_social } } } }
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}
	}

	#Campaign for military's interests
	campaigning_military_class = {
		picture = "campaigning_military_class"

		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			has_country_flag = show_campaigning_decision
			ai = no
			
			#Every gov type can do this
			
			#Has the required pop type
			OR = { has_pop_type = officers has_pop_type = soldiers }
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
			OR = { # Available only during elections for democratic govs
				AND = {
					OR = {
						government = socialist_democracy
						government = democracy
						government = democracy1
						government = hms_government
						government = hms_government1
						government = sar_government
						government = colonial_government
						government = mandate_government
					}
					election = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						government = socialist_democracy
						government = democracy
						government = democracy1
						government = hms_government
						government = hms_government1
						government = sar_government
						government = colonial_government
						government = mandate_government
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect = {
		
			#Timer
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = no } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 365 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = yes } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 31 } }
			}
			
			#Pacifists gain consciousness
			any_pop = {
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = 3
					issue = pacifism
				}
			}
			
			#Boost Jingoism
			any_pop = {
				dominant_issue = {
					value = jingoism
					factor = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			#Boost ideology support
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = officers type = soldiers } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = no } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = no } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Reduce ideology support in rural towns
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = {is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { location = { is_state_capital = yes } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = communist_social } } } }

	#Campaign for primary culture
	campaigning_primary_culture = {
		picture = "campaigning_primary_culture"

		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			has_country_flag = show_campaigning_decision
			ai = no
			
			#Every gov type can do this
			
			#Has either residency or limited citizenship
			OR = { citizenship_policy = residency citizenship_policy = limited_citizenship }
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
			OR = { # Available only during elections for democratic govs
				AND = {
					OR = {
						government = socialist_democracy
						government = democracy
						government = democracy1
						government = hms_government
						government = hms_government1
						government = sar_government
						government = colonial_government
						government = mandate_government
					}
					election = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						government = socialist_democracy
						government = democracy
						government = democracy1
						government = hms_government
						government = hms_government1
						government = sar_government
						government = colonial_government
						government = mandate_government
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect = {
		
			#Timer
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = no } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 365 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = yes } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 31 } }
			}
			
			#Majority races are pleased
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_culture_group = THIS }
				militancy = -2
				consciousness = -2
			}
			
			#Minority races get angry
			any_pop = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
				militancy = 2
				consciousness = 2
			}
			
			#Progressive and liberals are not happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = liberal
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}
			
			#Gain negative international attention
			any_country = {
				limit = { is_vassal = no citizenship_policy = full_citizenship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = -10 }
			}
			
			#Boost ideology support from culture group
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Reduce ideology support for non culture groups
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = communist } } } }

			has_country_flag = desecularized

			religious_policy = moralism
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }

				AND = {

						government = democracy

						government = hms_government1
						government = sar_government
						government = colonial_government
						government = mandate_government
					}
				}
			}

			}

			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_state_religion = yes }
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					issue = moralism
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = -2
					issue = moralism
				}
			}
			
			#Non state religion pops are angry
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_state_religion = no }
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					issue = secularized
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = 2
					issue = secularized
				}
				
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					issue = pro_atheism
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = 2
					issue = pro_atheism
				}
			}
			
			#Progressive and liberals are not happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = liberal

					factor = 2
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = liberal } } } }

				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = -2
					issue = pro_atheism
				}
			}
			
			#Non state religion pops are angry
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_state_religion = no }
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					issue = moralism
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = 2
					issue = moralism
				}
			}
			
			#Progressive and liberals are happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -1
					ideology = liberal
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -1
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}
			
			#Boost ideology support from culture group
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Reduce ideology support for non culture groups
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { has_pop_religion = secularism } } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = communist_social } } } }
			
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}
	}
	#Campaign for independence
	campaigning_independence = {
		picture = "campaigning_independence"

		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			has_country_flag = show_campaigning_decision
			ai = no
			
			#Every vassal gov type can do this
			is_vassal = yes
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
		}
		effect = {
		
			#Timer
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = no } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 365 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = yes } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 31 } }
			}
			
			#Nationalist, populist and communist are happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -3
					ideology = nationalist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					ideology = populist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					ideology = communist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					ideology = communist_social
				}
			}
			
			#Overlord is not pleased
			overlord = {
				relation = { who = THIS value = -20 }
			}
			
			#Increase nationalist support amongst primary culture
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = populist } } } }
			
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_global_flag = blocsenabled NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_global_flag = blocsenabled NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Boost ideology support for non culture groups
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { OR = { is_primary_culture = yes is_accepted_culture = yes } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist_social } } } }
			
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}

			NOT = { OR = { ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } }
		}

			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
		}

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = progressive } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = middle } ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = middle } ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Reduce ideology support for the rich
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = -0.10 value = communist_social } } } }
			
		}

			factor = 1 
		}

	#Dictatorship bribes - Reformists
	campaigning_dictatorship_reformists = {
		picture = "campaigning_dictatorship_reformists"

		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_civil_decisions }
			has_country_flag = show_campaigning_decision
			ai = no
			
			#Dictatorships only
			NOT = { OR = { government = socialist_democracy government = democracy government = democracy1 government = hms_government government = hms_government1 government = sar_government government = colonial_government government = mandate_government } }
			
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
		}
		effect = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 180 }
			
			#Hardliners get angry
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = conservative
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = traditionalist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = nationalist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = conservative
				}
			}
			
			#Increase UH support
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { NOT = { political_opinions = ruling_party_opinion } } }
				owner = { upper_house = { ideology = liberal value = 0.15 } }
			}

			#Boost liberal support amongst the elites
			any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = bureaucrats type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = liberal } }
			any_pop = { limit = { OR = { type = bureaucrats type = aristocrats } } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = progressive } }
			
			#Increase reactionary support amongst the military
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = officers } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = officers } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = officers } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = officers } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = conservative } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = officers } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = officers } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { type = officers } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Reformers are happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					ideology = liberal
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}
			
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}
	}

	#Hide/Show Economic Decisions
	hide_economy_decisions = {
		picture = "hide_economy_decisions"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions }
		}
		
		allow = { }
		
		effect = {
			set_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions
		}
		
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 0
		}
		
	}
	show_economy_decisions = {
		picture = "show_economy_decisions"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions
		}
		
		allow = { }
		
		effect = {
			clr_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions
		}
		
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	exportfocus = {
		picture = "exportfocus"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions }
			war = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = exportfocus }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = importfocus }
		}

		allow = {
			OR = { ai = no is_greater_power = yes is_secondary_power = yes }
		}

		effect = {
			
			set_country_flag = exportfocus
		any_owned = { limit = { is_colonial = no } add_province_modifier = { name = exportfocus duration = -1 } }
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}
	}
	importfocus = {
		picture = "importfocus"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions }

			NOT = { has_country_flag = importfocus }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = exportfocus }
		}
		allow = {

		}

			set_country_flag = importfocus

				limit = { is_colonial = no } 
				add_province_modifier = { name = importsubstitutionfocus duration = -1 } 
			}
		}

		picture = "changefocus"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions }
			war = no
			OR = { has_country_flag = importfocus has_country_flag = exportfocus } 
		}
		alert = no
		
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = south_american_isi }
			OR = { has_country_flag = importfocus has_country_flag = exportfocus } 
			OR = { ai = no AND = { is_secondary_power = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = exportfocus } } AND = { is_greater_power = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = exportfocus } } } 
		}
		effect = {
			clr_country_flag = importfocus
			clr_country_flag = exportfocus

			remove_country_modifier = spchigh
			remove_country_modifier = spcmedium
			remove_country_modifier = spclow
			remove_country_modifier = spcno
			clr_country_flag = spchigh
			clr_country_flag = spcmedium
			clr_country_flag = spclow
			clr_country_flag = spcno

			any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = importsubstitutionfocus }
			any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = exportfocus }
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
	}

	overlord_loan = {

		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions }

			is_greater_power = no

				part_of_sphere = yes
				is_vassal = yes
			}

			OR = {
				overlord = { NOT = { has_country_flag = stop_loan } AND = { is_vassal = no money = 1000000 } }
				any_greater_power = { AND = { is_sphere_leader_of = THIS money = 1000000 } }
			}

			#Did not take an overlord loan recently
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = overlord_loan_requested }

		}

							NOT = { has_province_modifier = spez }
							is_state_capital = yes
						}
					}
				}
				relation = { who = THIS value = 50 }
				country_event = 1410125
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	start_trade_war = {
		picture = "start_trade_war"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = trade_war_initiator }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = conceded_trade_war }
			rank = 3
			NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = juche }
		}
		alert = no
		allow = {
			war = no
			
			#Must have a large economy
			industrial_score = 1000
			
			election = no

			any_greater_power = { rank = 3 NOT = { has_country_modifier = conceded_trade_war } NOT = { has_country_modifier = juche } NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } } }

			OR = { ai = no ruling_party_ideology = populist }
		}

		effect = {

			add_country_modifier = { name = trade_war_tariffs duration = -1 }

			any_country = { 
				limit = { is_vassal = no is_greater_power = no NOT = { has_country_modifier = juche } } 
				relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } 
			}

			set_country_flag = trade_war_initiator

			set_global_flag = trade_war

			any_country = { 
				limit = { is_greater_power = yes NOT = { has_country_modifier = juche } NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } } } 
				country_event = 1512345 #Trade War declared
			}
			
			#Liberals are angry
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 3
					ideology = liberal
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 3
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}
			#Populists are happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -3
					ideology = populist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -3
					ideology = nationalist
				}
			}

		}

		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}

	}
	end_trade_war = {
		picture = "end_trade_war"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_economy_decisions }
			has_global_flag = trade_war
			has_country_flag = trade_war_initiator
		}

		allow = {
			election = no

			OR = { 
				ai = no 
				NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = populist }
				is_greater_power = no
				has_country_modifier = juche
				has_country_modifier = conceded_trade_war

				NOT = { any_greater_power = { rank = 3 NOT = { has_country_modifier = conceded_trade_war } NOT = { has_country_modifier = juche } NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } NOT = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } } } }
			}

		}

		effect = {

			remove_country_modifier = trade_war_tariffs

			clr_global_flag = trade_war
			clr_country_flag = trade_war_initiator

			#In case more than one GP declared a Trade War
			random_owned = {
				owner = { any_country = { limit = { is_greater_power = yes has_country_flag = trade_war_initiator } set_global_flag = trade_war } }
			}

			any_country = { 
				limit = { is_greater_power = yes NOT = { has_country_modifier = juche } } 
				country_event = 1512344 #Trade War Ended
			}
			
			#Liberals are happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -3
					ideology = liberal
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -3
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}
			#Populists are angry
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 3
					ideology = populist
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 3
					ideology = nationalist
				}
			}

		}

		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}

	}

	#Hide/Show Vassal Decisions
	hide_vassal_decisions = {
		picture = "hide_vassal_decisions"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			ai = no
			num_of_vassals = 1
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_vassal_decisions }
		}
		
		allow = { war = no }
		
		effect = {
			set_country_flag = hide_vassal_decisions
		}
		
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 0
		}
		
	}
	show_vassal_decisions = {
		picture = "show_vassal_decisions"
		alert = no
		potential = {
			ai = no
			num_of_vassals = 1
			has_country_flag = hide_vassal_decisions
		}
		
		allow = { }
		
		effect = {
			clr_country_flag = hide_vassal_decisions
		}
		
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	changevts = {
		picture = "changevts"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_vassal_decisions }
			num_of_vassals = 1
			OR = { 
				has_country_modifier = vtshigh
				has_country_modifier = vtsmedium
				has_country_modifier = vtslow 
			}
		}
		alert = no
		allow = {
			war = no
			election = no
			
			OR = { 
				ai = no 
				AND = { has_country_modifier = vtslow NOT = { OR = { economic_policy = state_capitalism economic_policy = planned_economy economic_policy = planned_economy1 } } } 
				AND = { has_country_modifier = vtsmedium NOT = { economic_policy = interventionism } } 
				AND = { has_country_modifier = vtshigh NOT = { economic_policy = laissez_faire } } 
			}
			
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = law_changed_by_force }
		}
		effect = {			
			remove_country_modifier = vtshigh
			remove_country_modifier = vtsmedium
			remove_country_modifier = vtslow
			clr_country_flag = vtshigh
			clr_country_flag = vtsmedium
			clr_country_flag = vtslow
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	vtslow = { #Tributary system for vassals
		picture = "vtslow"
		potential = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_vassal_decisions }
			num_of_vassals = 1
			NOT = { 
				OR = { 
					has_country_modifier = vtshigh
					has_country_modifier = vtsmedium
					has_country_modifier = vtslow 
				} 
			}
		}
		allow = {
			war = no
			OR = { ai = no economic_policy = state_capitalism economic_policy = planned_economy economic_policy = planned_economy1 }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = law_changed_by_force }
			NOT = { colonial_nation = yes }
		}
		effect = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = vtslow duration = -1 }
			set_country_flag = vtslow
			
			add_country_modifier = { name = law_changed_by_force duration = 400 }
			
			any_country = {
				limit = { vassal_of = THIS }
				any_pop = {
					militancy = 5
					consciousness = 5
				}
			}
			
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			factor = 1 
		}
	}
	vtsmedium = { #Financing autonomous states
		picture = "vtsmedium"

				OR = {

	vassal_interactions = {

    }
	annex_vassal_cores = {
